accordance with Securities and Exchange Commission Release No.&nbsp;33-8216,
the following information, which is intended to be furnished under Item 12,
&#147;Results of Operations and Financial Condition,&#148; is instead being furnished under
Item 9, &#147;Regulation FD Disclosure.&#148; This information shall not be deemed
&#147;filed&#148; for purposes of Section&nbsp;18 of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934,
as amended (the &#147;Exchange Act&#148;), or incorporated by reference in any filing
under the Securities Act of 1933, as amended, or the Exchange Act, except as
shall be expressly set forth by specific reference in such a filing.</font></p>

July&nbsp;16, 2003, Apple Computer,&nbsp;Inc. (&#147;Apple&#148;) issued a press release
regarding Apple&#146;s financial results for its third fiscal quarter ended June 28,
2003 and a related data sheet. A copy of Apple&#146;s press release is attached
hereto as Exhibit&nbsp;99.1 and a copy of the related data sheet is attached
hereto as Exhibit&nbsp;99.2.</font></p>

<div style="font-family:'Times New Roman';">



<p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Exhibit&nbsp;99.1</font></b></p>



<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>



<h2 style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:auto;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Apple Reports

Third Quarter Results</font></b></h2>



<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>



<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>



<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">CUPERTINO, California&#151;July 16,

2003&#151;Apple&#174; today announced financial results for its fiscal 2003 third quarter

ended June 28, 2003. For the quarter, the Company posted a net profit of $19

million, or $.05 per diluted share. These results compare to a net profit of

$32 million, or $.09 per diluted share, in the year-ago quarter. Revenues for

the quarter were $1.545 billion, up 8 percent from the year-ago quarter and up

5 percent sequentially, and gross margins were 27.7 percent, up from 27.4

percent in the year-ago quarter. International sales accounted for 39 percent

of the quarter&#146;s revenues.</font></p>



<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>



<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Apple shipped 771 thousand

Macintosh&#174; units during the quarter.</font></p>



<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>



<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;This was a great new product

quarter for Apple, starting with the iTunes Music Store and the new

third-generation iPods, and ending with the announcement of the Power Mac G5

and the developer preview of Panther, the fourth major release of Mac OS X,&#148;

said Steve Jobs, Apple&#146;s CEO.&#160; &#147;Customer

response to our new products has been very strong, and this quarter we are

focused on delivering Power Mac G5s beginning in August and finishing Panther

for release later this year.&#148;</font></p>



<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>



<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;We are very proud to have

exceeded our revenue target for the third quarter despite the difficult

economic backdrop,&#148; said Fred Anderson, Apple&#146;s CFO. &#147;We continue to be pleased

with our working capital management and our ability to increase cash which

totals over $4.5 billion.&#160; Looking ahead

to the fourth quarter of 2003, we expect an increase in revenues and a slight

increase in earnings relative to the June quarter.&#148;</font></p>



<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>



<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Apple ignited the personal

computer revolution in the 1970s with the Apple II and reinvented the personal

computer in the 1980s with the Macintosh. Apple is committed to bringing the

best personal computing experience to students, educators, creative

professionals and consumers around the world through its innovative hardware,

software and Internet offerings.</font></p>



<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>



<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Apple will provide live

streaming of its Q3 2003 financial results conference call utilizing

QuickTime&#153;, Apple&#146;s standards-based technology for live and on-demand audio and

video streaming. The live webcast will begin at 2:30 p.m. PT on Wednesday, July

16, 2003 at http://www.apple.com/quicktime/qtv/earningsq303/ and will also be

available for replay. The QuickTime player is available free for Macintosh and

Windows users at www.apple.com/quicktime.</font></p>



<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>



<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">This press release contains

forward-looking statements about future revenues, profit, and products.&#160; These statements involve risks and

uncertainties and actual results may differ. Potential risks and uncertainties

include continued competitive pressures in the marketplace; the effect

competitive and economic factors and the Company&#146;s reaction to them may have on

consumer and business buying decisions with respect to the Company&#146;s products;

the ability of the Company to make timely delivery of new programs, products

and successful technological innovations to the marketplace; the continued

availability of certain components and services essential to the Company&#146;s

business currently obtained by the Company from sole or limited sources;

possible disruption in commercial activities caused by terrorist activity and

armed conflict, such as changes in logistics and security arrangements, and

reduced end-user purchases relative to expectations; possible disruption in

commercial activity as a result of Severe Acute Respiratory Syndrome (SARS);

risks associated with the Company&#146;s retail initiative including significant

investment cost, uncertain consumer acceptance and potential impact on existing

reseller relationships; the effect that the Company&#146;s dependency on

manufacturing and logistics services provided by third-parties may have on the

quality or quantity of products manufactured; and the ability of the Company to

successfully evolve its operating system and attract sufficient Macintosh

developers. More information on potential factors that could affect the

Company&#146;s financial results is included from time to time in the Company&#146;s public

reports filed with the SEC, including the Company&#146;s Form 10-K for the fiscal

year 2002 and the Company&#146;s Form 10-Q for the quarter ended June 28, 2003 to be

filed with the SEC.</font></p>



<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>





<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">



<hr size="2" width="100%" noshade color="gray" align="left">



</font></div>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">CONSOLIDATED

  <td width="64%" valign="bottom" style="border:none;padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:64.74%;">
